    <script type="text/javascript">

        function AddPlayers(sender, eventArgs) {

            var listBox = $find("LeaderBoard1_rdPlayers");

            listBox.trackChanges();

            var selectedItem = eventArgs.get_item();
            var selectedItemText = selectedItem != null ? selectedItem.get_text() : sender.get_text();
            var selectedItemValue = selectedItem != null ? selectedItem.get_value() : sender.get_value();

            var item = new Telerik.Web.UI.RadListBoxItem();

            item.set_text(selectedItemText);
            item.set_value(selectedItemValue);

            if (selectedItemValue != '') {
                listBox.get_items().add(item);
                item.scrollIntoView();
                listBox.commitChanges();
                sender.set_text('');
            }

            return false;
        }

        function ShowHide() {
            var panel = document.getElementById('filterspan');

            if (panel.style.display == 'none') {
                panel.style.display = 'block';
            }
            else {
                panel.style.display = 'none';
            }

        }

    </script>
